## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="f2d2d-1190">Атрибуты Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f2d2d-1190">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f2d2d-1191">Этот класс содержит следующие атрибуты для Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f2d2d-1191">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
